|-

|-

|-

|-
| colspan="3" | null_spawn_chance || Default 0. 0.0 - 1.0 (0 to 100%) chance category will NOT spawn even if it is picked by the anomaly die roll. Used to make categories for unusual objects (e.g. black holes) actually rare. || Optional || Float
|-
| colspan="3" | max_once || default NO, if true will spawn category only once per empire || Optional || yes/no
|-
| colspan="3" | max_once_global || default NO, if true will spawn category only once per game || Optional || yes/no
|-
| colspan="3" | on_success || Picks anomaly event to fire; similar to random_list || Required || [[#event|<event>]] of subtype ship
